Testing code blocks in posts: ```rb def process_operation(op) case op.type when :plc_operation verify_handles(op.did, op.handles, op.pds_endpoint) when :plc_tombstone Handle.where(did: op.did).delete_all else log "PLC: unrecognized operation type: " + op.type end end ```

<img src="https://cdn.bsky.app/img/avatar/plain/did:plc:ukvymonlw4qm7e2klgcrgiu3/bafkreid5kolaksmzpbmxgswfbg7htqv4grer2y3lpyee5s2ymgezyjscye" class="bsky-avatar">

<br><small>2026-06-30</small>
</div>
</div>

<div class="bsky-content" markdown="1">

Found a bug in Bluesky's own atproto: the BCP 47 language-tag regex rejected valid tags whose private-use subtag uses an uppercase X (X-fr-CH). RFC 5646 makes those case-insensitive. Opened a small fix (x to [xX]) with a regression test. https://github.com/bluesky-social/atproto/pull/5169







</div>
